	&lt;span&gt;For more details on MIDI 2.0,&amp;nbsp;see this article on the site.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ebd-block  &quot; data-type=&quot;links&quot; &gt;&lt;div class=&quot;media-table&quot;&gt;

		&lt;/a&gt;

			&lt;h4 class=&quot;media-heading&quot;&gt;
				&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.midi.org/articles-old/midi-manufacturers-association-mma-adopts-midi-capability-inquiry-midi-ci-specification&quot; data-preview-title=&quot;&quot;&gt;MIDI Manufacturers Association (MMA) Adopts MIDI Capability Inquiry (MIDI-CI) Specification. - &amp;nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;
			&lt;/h4&gt;

			&lt;div class=&quot;media-content&quot; data-preview-content=&quot;&quot; data-gramm_id=&quot;a7f6d9a2-9cbb-480a-d3d4-dcf1dbd55198&quot; data-gramm=&quot;true&quot; spellcheck=&quot;false&quot; data-gramm_editor=&quot;true&quot;&gt;More Details on MIDI-CI and MIDI 2.0.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;grammarly-btn&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;_1BN1N Kzi1t BD-0J _7_mnr MoE_1 _2DJZN&quot; style=&quot;z-index: 2; transform: translate(215.75px, 55px);&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;_1HjH7&quot;&gt;&lt;div title=&quot;Protected by Grammarly&quot; class=&quot;_3qe6h&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/grammarly-btn&gt;

			&lt;div class=&quot;media-link&quot;&gt;
				&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.midi.org/articles-old/midi-manufacturers-association-mma-adopts-midi-capability-inquiry-midi-ci-specification&quot; data-preview-link=&quot;&quot;&gt;https://www.midi.org/articles-old/midi-manufacturers-association-mma-adopts-midi-capability-inquiry-midi-ci-specification&lt;/a&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ebd-block  &quot; data-type=&quot;text&quot; &gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt;FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt;The MIDI Manufacturers Association (MMA) and the Association of Music Electronics Industry (AMEI) announce MIDI 2.0&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s2&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s2&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt;&lt;sup data-redactor-tag=&quot;sup&quot;&gt;TM&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt; Prototyping&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt;Los Angeles, CA, January 18, 2019&lt;/b&gt; &ndash; The MIDI Manufacturers Association (MMA) and AMEI (the Japanese MIDI association) have finalized the core features and name for the next generation MIDI protocol: MIDI 2.0. Member companies are currently working together to develop prototypes based on a jointly developed, feature-complete, draft specification. A members-only plugfest to test compatibility between some early MIDI 2.0 prototypes is planned for Winter NAMM 2019. Participating companies include Ableton/Cycling &#039;74, Art+Logic, Bome Software, Google, &lt;g class=&quot;gr_ gr_29 gr-alert gr_spell gr_inline_cards gr_run_anim ContextualSpelling&quot; id=&quot;29&quot; data-gr-id=&quot;29&quot;&gt;imitone&lt;/g&gt;, Native Instruments, Roland, ROLI, Steinberg, TouchKeys, and Yamaha.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;As with MIDI 1.0, AMEI and the MMA are working closely together and sharing code to streamline the prototype development process. Prototyping is planned to continue during 2019 as the associations work together on MIDI 2.0 launch plans, including exploring the development of a MIDI 2.0 logo and self-certification program for MMA and AMEI member companies.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;During the prototyping phase, the proposed MIDI 2.0 specification is available only to MMA and AMEI members, because the prototyping process may trigger minor enhancements to the specification. Once a final specification is adopted, it will join the current MIDI specifications as a free download on www.midi.org.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;The MIDI 2.0 initiative updates MIDI with auto-configuration, new DAW/web integrations, extended resolution, increased expressiveness, and tighter timing -- all while maintaining a high priority on backward compatibility. This major update of MIDI paves the way for a new generation of advanced interconnected MIDI devices, while still preserving interoperability with the millions of existing MIDI 1.0 devices. One of the core goals of the MIDI 2.0 initiative is to also enhance the MIDI 1.0 feature set whenever possible.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;All companies that develop MIDI products are encouraged to join the MMA to participate in the future development of the specification, and to keep abreast of other developments in MIDI technology.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt;About the MIDI Manufacturers Association (MMA)&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;The MIDI Manufacturers Association is an international group of hardware and software companies working together to develop new MIDI specifications and promote MIDI technology. For more information on the MMA corporate membership, please visit &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.midi.org/lists/lt.php?tid=fUxSWl8NAQIIUhxSAAQBSQYGUVUVW1ELWEgAWFZUAwYMAlIJCwFEWg9bAAdTAQdJUAcFVBUNAlJZSFMDVlUcCQdWXFgIXAwGDFYETFRTBAAKUQQGFQEJBVJIBlRRAxwJVwNcFAkJDQBYVQkBWgkEUg&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s3&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s3&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;www.midi.org/about-the-mma&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s1&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s1&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;The MMA also supports The MIDI Association, a growing, global community of over 18,000 people who work, play, and create with MIDI technology at &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.midi.org/lists/lt.php?tid=fUwAXAgPWlUJWhxWAlUOSQYNClQVAQNQAkhQAgUCBwIHCF1fDwtEWg9bAAdTAQdJUAcFVBUNAlJZSFMDVlUcCQdWXFgIXAwGDFYETFRTBAAKUQQGFQEJBVJIBlRRAxwJVwNcFAkJDQBYVQkBWgkEUg&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s3&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s3&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;www.midi.org&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. To stay up to date with the latest MIDI news and stories, and to access current MIDI specifications and receive the MIDI Association&#039;s MIDI Message newsletter, sign up for free &lt;g class=&quot;gr_ gr_31 gr-alert gr_gramm gr_inline_cards gr_run_anim Punctuation only-del replaceWithoutSep&quot; id=&quot;31&quot; data-gr-id=&quot;31&quot;&gt;at:&lt;/g&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.midi.org/lists/lt.php?tid=fUxWDwAACwJdURxUUwlTSQYFVAYVAABWWEgCWAQHBlJUVgcLCgpEWg9bAAdTAQdJUAcFVBUNAlJZSFMDVlUcCQdWXFgIXAwGDFYETFRTBAAKUQQGFQEJBVJIBlRRAxwJVwNcFAkJDQBYVQkBWgkEUg&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s3&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s3&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;www.midi.org/midi-signup&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b data-redactor-tag=&quot;b&quot;&gt;Press Contact: &lt;/b&gt;&lt;span&gt;Tom White, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;mailto:press@midi.org&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;s3&quot; data-redactor-tag=&quot;span&quot; data-redactor-class=&quot;s3&quot; data-verified=&quot;redactor&quot;&gt;press@midi.org&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;",
